function findKeys(obj, keyPattern, pathArr=[], out=[]){
 if(!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return out;
 for (const [k,v] of Object.entries(obj)){
   const p = pathArr.concat(k);
   if(keyPattern.test(k)) out.push(p.join('.'));
   if (typeof v === 'object') findKeys(v,keyPattern,p,out);
 }
 return out;
}

var candidateAnchors2 = uniqAnchors1.filter(x => /one\s*piece|onepiece|swim dress/i.test(x.text));
async function fetchProductSummary2(href){
  const res = await fetch(href);
  const html = await res.text();
  const m = html.match(/<script[^>]+id="__NEXT_DATA__"[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/script>/);
  if(!m) return {href, error:'no next data'};
  const data = JSON.parse(m[1]);
  const p = data.props?.pageProps?.product;
  if(!p) return {href, error:'no product'};
  const variants = (p.variants || []).map(v => {
    const pr = v.price || {};
    const priceObj = pr.price || v.price?.price;
    const rrpObj = pr.rrp || v.price?.rrp;
    const amount = parseFloat(priceObj?.amount ?? priceObj?.displayValue?.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,'') ?? 'NaN');
    const rrp = parseFloat(rrpObj?.amount ?? rrpObj?.displayValue?.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,'') ?? 'NaN');
    return {
      sku: v.sku,
      title: v.title,
      inStock: v.inStock,
      selectedOptions: v.selectedOptions,
      productOptions: v.productOptions,
      size: v.selectedOptions?.Size || v.productOptions?.Size || (v.title?.match(/ - ([^-]+)$/)?.[1]),
      amount, rrp,
      discountPct: (rrp && amount) ? (rrp-amount)/rrp*100 : null
    };
  });
  const mainPrice = p.price || p.defaultVariant?.price;
  return {
    title:p.title, href, productSku:p.sku, inStockSizes:p.inStockSizes, sizes:p.sizes, selectedOptions:p.selectedOptions,
    variants,
    maxDiscountPct: Math.max(...variants.map(v=>v.discountPct ?? -1)),
    hasLarge: variants.some(v => v.inStock && /^(L|Large)$/i.test(String(v.size||'').trim())) || (p.inStockSizes||[]).some(s=>/^(L|Large)$/i.test(String(s).trim()))
  };
}
var summaries2 = await Promise.all(candidateAnchors2.map(x => fetchProductSummary2(x.href).catch(e=>({href:x.href,error:e.message}))));
var sortedSummaries2 = summaries2.map((s,i)=>({order:i+1, listingText:candidateAnchors2[i].text, ...s})).sort((a,b)=>(b.maxDiscountPct??-1)-(a.maxDiscountPct??-1));
